ACQUISITION OF LANDS
FORM C
[See Rule 7]
NOTICE UNDER SUB-SECTION(1) OF SECTION 3 OF THE TAMIL NADU ACQUISITION OF LAND FOR 
INDUSTRIAL PURPOSES ACT, 1997
 
(cla-sip/2024/40/07/03/0001)
No.VI(1)/776(b-1)/2024.
 The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be 
acquired for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park and it having already been decided that 
the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by 
the Managing Director, SIPCOT.  The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu 
Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
 Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 11.3600 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park.


2	
TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY
 The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvallur and Special Tahsildar(LA), Unit , 
Tiruvallur which may be inspected on any day during office hours.

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY
(CLA-SIP/2024/40/03/07/0001)
No.VI(1)/776(b-4)/2024.
 The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be 
acquired for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park and it having already been decided that 
the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by 
the Managing Director, SIPCOT, Chennai. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the 
Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
 Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 9.3100 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park.
 The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvallur and Special Tahsildar(LA), Unit, 
Tiruvallur which may be inspected on any day during office hours.

Total extent to be acquired : 9.3100 (Hectares)
(CLA-SIP/2024/40/08/07/0001)
No.VI(1)/776(b-5)/2024.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be 
acquired for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park and it having already been decided that 
the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by 
the Managing Director, SIPCOT, Chennai. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the 
Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 11.0650 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvallur and Special Tahsildar(LA), Unit , 
Tiruvallur which may be inspected on any day during office hours.
The Schedule
Tiruvallur District, Gummidipoondi Taluk, Madarpakkam Village.

No.VI(1)/776(b-6)/2024.
       The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below 
to be acquired for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park and it having already been 
decided that the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or 
managed by the Managing Director, SIPCOT. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the 
Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)


	
TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY	
31
NOTICE
 Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Lands for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 10.9250 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park.
 The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvallur and Special Tahsildar(LA), Unit , 
Tiruvallur may be inspected on any day during office hours.

(CLA-SIP/2024/40/01/08/0001)
No.VI(1)/776(b-7)/2024.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be 
acquired for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park and it having already been decided that 
the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by 
the Managing Director, SIPCOT, Chennai. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the 
Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
 Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Lands for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 9.5400 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park.
 The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvallur and Special Tahsildar(LA), Unit, 
Tiruvallur may be inspected on any day during office hours.

No.VI(1)/776(b-8)/2024.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be 
acquired for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park and it having already been decided that 
the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by 
the Managing Director, SIPCOT, Chennai. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil 
Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Lands for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 10.3400 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvallur and Special Tahsildar(LA), Unit 
,Tiruvallur may be inspected on any day during office hours.
